**Candidate 31:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + T*c2*log(c3*exp(c4*epsilon)+1) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon*exp(T*c8)`. `exp(T*c8)` is not `exp(-c/T)`. No T². [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 32:** No T dependence (unless c2 involves T... no, c2 is a constant). Actually wait - `c0*exp(c1/(c2+epsilon)) + c3*exp(c4*exp(c5*epsilon))`. No T at all. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 33:** Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 34:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2+epsilon)) + c3*exp(c4/(T+c5)) + c6*(c7*exp(c8*epsilon)+1)**c9`. Has exp(c4/(T+c5)) which is Arrhenius-like. But missing T² terms, epsilon³. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 35:** Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 36:** All terms divided by `(c1+epsilon)`. Multiplying through by `(c1+epsilon)`: `T*c0*epsilon² + T*c2*epsilon + T*c3 + T*c4*epsilon + c5*exp(c6*epsilon)*log(T*c7+1) + c8*epsilon + c9*epsilon*exp(c6*epsilon)*log(T*c7+1)`. Linear in T (log is not T²). [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 37:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon³ + c2*epsilon² + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)) + c9*epsilon`. Has epsilon³ ✓ but only linear in T. Missing T², exp(-c/T). [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 38:** Rational in epsilon, linear in T. No T². [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 39:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*log(T*c7+1) + c8))`. The sin(log(T)) term is complex but not T². [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 40:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon*exp(T*c5) + c6*exp(c7*sin(T*c8+c9))`. exp(T*c5) and sin(T*c8) are not T². [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 41:** Linear in T plus `1/(c9+epsilon)^5`. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 42:** Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 43:** Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 44:** Similar to 36. Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 45:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2 + T*c3*epsilon² + T*c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7 + c8*epsilon`. Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 46:** `T²*c0*epsilon + T*c1*epsilon + T*c2 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon³ + c6*|epsilon|^c7`. Has T²*epsilon ✓, T*epsilon ✓, epsilon³ ✓, epsilon ✓. The `|epsilon|^c7` with c7≈0.2144 and domain epsilon≥0 gives `epsilon^0.2144`. But GT needs `epsilon^0.2144 * exp(-c/T)`, not just `epsilon^0.2144`. The T*c2 term gives a T-dependent constant, not matching. Missing the Arrhenius factor. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 47:** Linear in T. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 48:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon³ + c5*epsilon*(T+c6)**c7`. If c7=2: `c5*epsilon*(T+c6)² = c5*epsilon*(T²+2c6*T+c6²)`. This gives `c5*epsilon*T² + 2*c5*c6*epsilon*T + c5*c6²*epsilon`. Combined with other terms: `T*(c0*epsilon+c1) + (c2+c5*c6²)*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon³ + c5*epsilon*T² + 2*c5*c6*epsilon*T`. 

Total: `c5*epsilon*T² + (c0+2*c5*c6)*epsilon*T + c1*T + c4*epsilon³ + (c2+c5*c6²)*epsilon + c3`.

GT: `1.336*epsilon*T² - 874.45*epsilon*T + 7.723*epsilon³ + 143088*epsilon + 36.659*epsilon^0.2144*exp(-9.916/T)`

Candidate 48 has: epsilon*T² ✓, epsilon*T ✓, epsilon³ ✓, epsilon ✓, T (extra but can set c1=0), constant (extra, set c3=0). But **missing** `epsilon^0.2144*exp(-c/T)`. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 49:** Linear in T (via log). [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 50:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon³ + c4*exp(c5*sin(T*c6+c7*epsilon+c8))`. The exp(sin(...)) term mixes T and epsilon in a transcendental way, cannot produce `epsilon^0.21*exp(-c/T)`. [NO MATCH]

None of the candidates contain the essential `epsilon^(fractional power) * exp(-constant/T)` Arrhenius-type term combined with `epsilon*T²` and `epsilon³`.
